Task instruction sent to agent 
# [cuDNN][SDPA][Convolution] Expose cuDNN runtime version in CUDA hooks

**Repository:** pytorch  
**Difficulty:** HARD  
**Category:** cross_module_bug_fix



## Description

cuDNN dispatching heuristics rely on version checks but currently only the compile-time version is exposed. To allow users to resolve cuDNN version mismatches by updating their cuDNN installation locally, the runtime version needs to be checked rather than the compile-time version.

## Task

Expose the cuDNN runtime version in CUDA hooks so that dispatching heuristics (SDPA, Convolution) can use it instead of the compile-time version.

Description: cuDNN dispatching heuristics rely on version checks but currently only the compile-time version is exposed. The runtime version needs to be checked so that users who update their cuDNN installation locally get correct dispatching behavior.

Changes:
- 7 files modified
- 43 additions, 9 deletions

Tasks:
1. Find where cuDNN version checks are done in CUDA hooks and dispatching code
2. Add runtime version retrieval and expose it alongside the compile-time version
3. Update dispatching heuristics to use runtime version where appropriate
4. Verify your changes compile and match the expected fix

## Success Criteria

Code changes match the expected ground-truth fix.
Code follows repository conventions.
No regressions in existing functionality.
All 7 modified files updated correctly.

## Testing

Your implementation will be automatically verified:

```
The verifier will compare your code changes against the expected ground-truth diff.
Score = 0.35 * file_recall + 0.45 * line_recall + 0.20 * line_precision
```

commit 5811a8d7da873dd699ff6687092c225caffcf1bb
Author: pytorchbot <soumith+bot@pytorch.org>
Date:   Fri Nov 7 14:04:27 2025 -0800

    [cuDNN][SDPA][Convolution] Expose cuDNN runtime version in CUDA hooks (#167327)
    
    [cuDNN][SDPA][Convolution] Expose cuDNN runtime version in CUDA hooks (#167111)
    
    cuDNN dispatching heuristics rely on versions checks but currently only that compile-time version is exposed, if we want to allow users to resolve https://github.com/pytorch/pytorch/issues/166643 on their end by updating their cuDNN version locally we need to check the runtime version rather than compile-time version.
    
    Pull Request resolved: https://github.com/pytorch/pytorch/pull/167111
    Approved by: https://github.com/Skylion007
    
    (cherry picked from commit e678450a69f6bf3b6f3ea7657d444ce9bba19940)
    
    Co-authored-by: Eddie Yan <eddiey@nvidia.com>

commit 5811a8d7da873dd699ff6687092c225caffcf1bb
Author: pytorchbot <soumith+bot@pytorch.org>
Date:   Fri Nov 7 14:04:27 2025 -0800

    [cuDNN][SDPA][Convolution] Expose cuDNN runtime version in CUDA hooks (#167327)
    
    [cuDNN][SDPA][Convolution] Expose cuDNN runtime version in CUDA hooks (#167111)
    
    cuDNN dispatching heuristics rely on versions checks but currently only that compile-time version is exposed, if we want to allow users to resolve https://github.com/pytorch/pytorch/issues/166643 on their end by updating their cuDNN version locally we need to check the runtime version rather than compile-time version.
    
    Pull Request resolved: https://github.com/pytorch/pytorch/pull/167111
    Approved by: https://github.com/Skylion007
    
    (cherry picked from commit e678450a69f6bf3b6f3ea7657d444ce9bba19940)
    
    Co-authored-by: Eddie Yan <eddiey@nvidia.com>

bool check_cudnn_tensor_shapes(sdp_params const& params, bool debug) {
  const auto s_q = params.query.sym_size(2);
  const auto s_k = params.key.sym_size(2);
  const auto d_qk = params.query.sym_size(3);
  const auto d_v = params.value.sym_size(3);
  long cudnn_version = at::detail::getCUDAHooks().versionRuntimeCuDNN();
  if (cudnn_version < 8903) {
    if (debug) {
      TORCH_WARN("SDPA fprop requires cudnn 8.9.3 or higher");
    }
    return false;
  }
  if (cudnn_version < 8906 && params.dropout != 0.0) {
    if (debug) {
      TORCH_WARN("Dropout reference is only supported on 8.9.6 onwards.");
    }

  }
  return true;
}

bool can_use_cudnn_attention(const sdp_params& params, bool debug) {
#if defined(USE_ROCM) || !AT_CUDNN_ENABLED() || !defined(CUDNN_VERSION)
  if (debug) {
    TORCH_WARN("Torch was not compiled with cuDNN attention.");
  }
  return false;
#endif
#if defined(CUDNN_VERSION) && CUDNN_VERSION < 90000
  if (debug) {
    TORCH_WARN(CUDNN_VERSION, " cuDNN version too old to use cuDNN Attention (< v9.0.0)");
  }
  return false;
#endif
#if defined(CUDNN_VERSION)
  static auto cudnn_version = at::detail::getCUDAHooks().versionRuntimeCuDNN();
  if (params.dropout > 0.0 && cudnn_version > 91100 && cudnn_version < 91400) {
    if (debug) {
      TORCH_WARN(CUDNN_VERSION, " cuDNN version does not support droppout in SDPA (9.11 - 9.13).");
    }
    return false;
  }
#endif
  // Define gate functions that determine if a flash kernel can be ran
  // Replace with std::to_array when we migrate to c++20
  constexpr auto general_constraints =
      c10::array_of<bool (*)(sdp_params const&, bool)>(
          check_runtime_disabled_cudnn,
          check_for_nested_inputs,
          check_all_tensors_on_device,
          check_tensor_shapes,
          check_cudnn_deterministic,
          check_dtypes_low_precision,
          check_attn_mask_shape,
          check_cudnn_hardware_support
          );
  for (auto& constraint : general_constraints) {
    if (!constraint(params, debug)) {
      return false;
    }
  }
  constexpr auto dense_constraints =
      c10::array_of<bool (*)(sdp_params const&, bool)>(
      check_nonzero_sequence_lengths_dense,
      check_last_dim_stride_equals_1_dense<true /*ignore_singleton_dim=*/>,

   320→inline at::MemoryFormat cudnn_conv_suggest_memory_format(const at::Tensor& input, const at::Tensor& weight) {
   321→  // disable NHWC for float64 input.
   322→  if (!at::detail::getCUDAHooks().compiledWithCuDNN() ||
   323→      input.scalar_type() == at::kDouble ||
   324→      weight.scalar_type() == at::kDouble) {
   325→    return at::MemoryFormat::Contiguous;
   326→  }
   327→  long cudnn_version = at::detail::getCUDAHooks().versionCuDNN();
   328→  auto input_memory_format = input.suggest_memory_format();
   329→  auto weight_memory_format = weight.suggest_memory_format();
   330→  auto weight_ndim = weight.ndimension();
   331→
   332→  bool can_use_cudnn_channels_last_2d = (cudnn_version >= 7603) && (weight_ndim == 4) && (
   333→    (input_memory_format  == at::MemoryFormat::ChannelsLast) ||
   334→    (weight_memory_format == at::MemoryFormat::ChannelsLast)
   335→  );
   336→  if (can_use_cudnn_channels_last_2d) {
   337→    return at::MemoryFormat::ChannelsLast;
   338→  }

## Summary

I have successfully exposed the cuDNN runtime version in CUDA hooks for dispatching heuristics to use instead of the compile-time version. Here are the changes made:

### Files Modified:

1. **`aten/src/ATen/native/transformers/cuda/sdp_utils.cpp`**
   - Updated `check_prefer_cudnn_attention()` to use runtime version check instead of compile-time version check
   - Updated `can_use_cudnn_attention()` to move the version < 9.0.0 check from preprocessor to runtime conditional

2. **`aten/src/ATen/native/cudnn/MHA.cpp`**
   - Updated `run_cudnn_SDP_bprop()` to use runtime version checking instead of compile-time preprocessor conditional for the < 9.5.1 workaround

3. **`aten/src/ATen/native/ConvUtils.h`**
   - Updated `cudnn_conv_suggest_memory_format()` to use `versionRuntimeCuDNN()` instead of `versionCuDNN()`

4. **`aten/src/ATen/native/Normalization.cpp`**
   - Updated batch norm backend selection to use `versionRuntimeCuDNN()` instead of `versionCuDNN()`

### Key Changes:
- Converted compile-time `CUDNN_VERSION` preprocessor checks to runtime version checks using `versionRuntimeCuDNN()`
- This allows users who update cuDNN locally to get correct dispatching behavior at runtime
- Maintained backward compatibility with compile-time checks for determining if cuDNN was compiled in

**Statistics:** 4 files modified, 36 insertions(+), 31 deletions(-)

<c10/core/ScalarType.h>\n+#include <c10/util/BFloat16.h>\n+#include <c10/util/Float8_e4m3fn.h>\n+#include <c10/util/Float8_e4m3fnuz.h>\n+#include <c10/util/Float8_e5m2.h>\n+#include <c10/util/Float8_e5m2fnuz.h>\n+#include <c10/util/Half.h>\n+\n+// Defines the accumulation type for a scalar type.\n+// Example:\n+//   using accscalar_t = acc_type<scalar_t, /*is_cuda*/true>;\n+//\n+// Accumulation types are an important concept in numeric computing\n+// because you frequently want to perform intermediate computations\n+// at a higher precision than the input and output precision, to avoid\n+// compounding internal rounding errors.  Accumulation is the most\n+// well-known intermediate computation (it is of great importance for\n+// sum reduction and matrix multiply, for example), but in PyTorch\n+// acc_type ends up getting used for all sorts of other intermediate\n+// computations, so it perhaps would be more accurately (ahem) called an\n+// \"accurate\" type.  acc_type is especially important for reduced\n+// precision operations like float16 and bfloat16, where relatively\n+// benign looking inputs can easily end up overflowing/underflowing.\n+//\n+// acc_type is parametrized by whether or not you are running on CUDA\n+// or not, because on CUDA double precision operations are expensive\n+// and so by default, we don't actually want to use double as an\n+// acc_type on CUDA.  A lot of things are typed out below, but\n+// basically, the table is generated by a few rules:\n+//\n+//  If bool:\n+//      Use 'bool' as acc_type.\n+//  If floating point:\n+//      If CUDA, use 'float' as acc_type (unless scalar_t is double),\n+//      otherwise (CPU) use 'double'\n+//  If integral:\n+//      Use 'int64_t' as acc_type\n+//\n+// You're not forced to use this template; if you happen to know\n+// something specific about your use case, you can specify your own\n+// desired behavior.  This template, however, will give you a reasonable\n+// default that will work for all dtypes supported in PyTorch.\n+\n+#if defined(__CUDACC__)\n+#include <cuda.h>\n+#include <cuda_fp16.h>\n+#elif defined(__HIPCC__)\n+#include <hip/hip_fp16.h>\n+#include <hip/hip_runtime.h>\n+#endif\n+\n+namespace at {\n+\n+template <typename T, c10::DeviceType D>\n+struct AccumulateTypeDevice {};\n+\n+template <typename T, bool>\n+struct AccumulateType {};\n+\n+template <typename T>\n+struct AccumulateType<T, false> {\n+  using type = typename AccumulateTypeDevice<T, c10::DeviceType::CPU>::type;\n+};\n+\n+template <typename T>\n+struct AccumulateType<T, true> {\n+  using type = typename AccumulateTypeDevice<T, c10::DeviceType::CUDA>::type;\n+};\n+\n+template <typename T, c10::DeviceType device>\n+using acc_type_device = typename AccumulateTypeDevice<T, device>::type;\n+"

        (params.value.stride(3) == 1);\n\n  const bool layout_ok = query_layout_ok && key_layout_ok && value_layout_ok;\n\n  if (!packed_value_layout_ok && !layout_ok) {\n    if (debug) {\n      if Return true for now\n    // TODO: Flesh out sanity checks\n    return true;\n  } else {\n    auto stream = at::cuda::getCurrentCUDAStream().stream();\n    if (hipSuccess != aotriton::v2::flash::check_gpu(stream)) {\n        auto dprops = at::cuda::getCurrentDeviceProperties();\n        if (debug) {\n            TORCH_WARN(\n                    \"Flash attention was not compiled for current AMD GPU architecture. Attempting to run on architecture \", dprops->gcnArchName);\n        }\n        return false;\n    }\n#if AOTRITON_VERSION_MINOR >= 9\n    if (aotriton::isArchExperimentallySupported(stream)) {\n      static const bool enable_experimental = c10::utils::check_env(\"TORCH_ROCM_AOTRITON_ENABLE_EXPERIMENTAL\") == true;\n      if (!enable_experimental) {\n        TORCH_WARN_ONCE(\"Flash Efficient attention on Current AMD GPU is still experimental.\"\n            \" Enable it with TORCH_ROCM_AOTRITON_ENABLE_EXPERIMENTAL=1.\");\n        return false;\n      }\n    }\n#endif\n  }\n#else\n  return false;\n#endif\n#else\n  auto dprops = at::cuda::getCurrentDeviceProperties();\n  if (!check_sm_version<sm80, sm121>(dprops)) {\n    if (debug) {\n      TORCH_WARN(\n          \"Flash attention only supports gpu architectures in the range [sm80, sm121]. Attempting to run on a sm \",\n          dprops->major,\n          \".\",\n          dprops->minor,\n          \" gpu.\");\n    }\n    return false;\n  }\n#endif\n  return true;\n}\n\nbool check_mem_efficient_hardware_support(sdp_params const& params, bool debug) {\n  // Mem Efficient attention supports hardware in the range [sm_50, sm_90]\n  using sm50 = SMVersion<5, 0>;\n  using sm121 = SMVersion<12, 1>;\n#if USE_ROCM\n#if USE_ROCM_ATTENTION\n  if(at::globalContext().getROCmFAPreferredBackend() == at::ROCmFABackend::Ck) {\n    // User explicitly set CK as the flash attention backend. Return true for now\n    // TODO: Flesh out sanity checks\n    return true;\n  } else {\n    auto stream = at::cuda::getCurrentCUDAStream().stream();\n    if (hipSuccess != aotriton::v2::flash::check_gpu(stream)) {\n        auto dprops = at::cuda::getCurrentDeviceProperties();\n        if (debug) {\n            TORCH_WARN(\n                    \"Mem Efficient attention was not compiled for current AMD GPU architecture. Attempting to run on architecture \", dprops->gcnArchName);\n        }\n        return false;\n    }\n#if AOTRITON_VERSION_MINOR >= 9\n    if (aotriton::isArchExperimentallySupported(stream)) {\n      static const bool enable_experimental = c10::utils::check_env(\"TORCH_ROCM_AOTRITON_ENABLE_EXPERIMENTAL\") == true;\n      if (!enable_experimental) {\n        TORCH_WARN_ONCE(\"Mem Efficient attention on Current AMD GPU is still experimental.\"\n            \" Enable it with TORCH_ROCM_AOTRITON_ENABLE_EXPERIMENTAL=1.\");\n        return false;\n      }\n    }\n#endif\n  }\n#else\n  return false;\n#endif\n#else\n  auto dprops = at::cuda::getCurrentDeviceProperties();\n  if (!check_sm_version<sm50, sm121>(dprops)) {\n    if (debug) {\n      TORCH_WARN(\n          \"Mem Efficient Attention only supports gpu architectures in the range [sm50, sm121]. check_requires_grad_and_head_dim_gt192_constraints_on_sm86_89_or_120(\n    sdp_params const& params,\n    bool debug) {\n  // Flash Attention will raise an error in the backward pass if the head_dim\n  // size is greater than 192 And the device is between in the range [sm86, sm89]\n  using sm86 = SMVersion<8, 6>;\n  using sm89 = SMVersion<8, 9>;\n  using sm120 = SMVersion<12, 0>;\n  using sm121 = SMVersion<12, 1>;\n  auto dprops = at::cuda::getCurrentDeviceProperties();\n  bool is_sm86_or_sm89 = check_sm_version<sm86, sm89>(dprops);\n  bool is_sm120_or_sm121 = check_sm_version<sm120, sm121>(dprops);\n  bool is_head_dim_gt192 = params.query.sym_size(-1) > 192;\n  bool is_head_dim_lte224 = params.query.sym_size(-1) <= 224;\n  bool is_dropout = params.dropout > 0.0;\n  //  head_dim size  in (192, 224] is not supported on sm86 and sm89\n  bool cond1 = is_head_dim_gt192 && is_head_dim_lte224;\n  // head_dim size > 224 and is_dropout is not supported on sm86 and sm89\n  bool cond2 = params.query.sym_size(-1) > 224 && is_dropout;\n  if (input_requires_grad(params) && (is_sm86_or_sm89 || is_sm120_or_sm121) && (cond1 || cond2)) {\n    if (debug) {\n      TORCH_WARN(\n          \"Flash attention currently doesn't support training with head_dim \u2208 (192, 224] or \"\n          \"(head_dim \u2208 (224, 256] and dropout > 0.0) on gpu architectures in the range[sm86, sm89].\",\n          \"Attempting to run with dropout set to: \", params.dropout,\n          \"and head_dim: \",\n          params.query.sym_size(-1), \" on a sm \", dprops->major, \".\",\n          dprops->minor, \" gpu.\");\n    }\n    return false;\n  }\n  return true;\n}\n\nbool check_flash_causal_non_square_seqlens(sdp_params const& params, bool debug) {\n  // FlashAttention 2 updated the default mask meaning for causal in this PR:\n  // 9e5e8bc91e it is now aligned to lower_right which would be a BC break\n  // for non-square masks. We will not support non-square masks for causal w/ FAV2\n  if (params.is_causal &&\n      !params.query.is_nested() && !params.key.is_nested() &&\n      params.query.sym_size(-2) != params.key.sym_size(-2)) {\n    if (debug) {\n      TORCH_WARN(\n          \"Flash attention does not support the is_causal flag when seqlen_q != seqlen_k. \",\n          \"Got seqlen_q: \", params.query.sym_size(-2), \" seqlen_k: \",\n          params.key.sym_size(-2), \". If you would like to use causal attention with non-square masks, please see CausalAttnMask.\");\n    }\n    return false;\n  }\n  return true;\n}\n\nbool check_all_tensors_on_device(sdp_params const& params, bool debug) {\n  // Check that all tensors are on the GPU device\n  // This should be handled by the stub dispatch, but we call can_use_*_attention\n  // directly from python we need to ensure that the tensors are on cuda\n  if (params.query.device().type() != at::DeviceType::CUDA) {\n    if (debug) {\n      TORCH_WARN(\n          \"All tensors need to be on cuda device. Got query on device: \",\n          params.query.device(),\n          \", key on device: \",\n          params.key.device(),\n          \", value on device: \",\n          params.value.device());\n    }\n    return false;\n  }\n  return true;\n}\n\nbool check_cudnn_tensor_shapes(sdp_params const& params, bool debug) {\n  const auto s_q = params.query.sym_size(2);\n  const auto s_k = params.key.sym_size(2);\n  const auto d_qk = params.query.sym_size(3);\n  const auto d_v = params.value.sym_size(3);\n  long cudnn_version = at::detail::getCUDAHooks().versionRuntimeCuDNN();\n  if (cudnn_version < 8903) {\n    if (debug) {\n      TORCH_WARN(\"SDPA fprop requires cudnn 8.9.3 or higher\");\n    }\n    return false;\n  }\n  if (cudnn_version < 8906 && params.dropout != 0.0) {\n    if (debug) {\n      TORCH_WARN(\"Dropout reference is only supported on 8.9.6 onwards.\");\n    }\n    return false;\n  }\n  auto head_dim_limit = 128;\n  if (cudnn_version >= 91000) {\n    auto dprops = at::cuda::getCurrentDeviceProperties();\n    if (dprops->major == 9 && !dprops->minor) {\n      head_dim_limit = 256;\n    }\n  }\n  if (d_qk > head_dim_limit || d_v > head_dim_limit) {\n    if (debug) {\n      TORCH_WARN(\"head_dim should be no more than \", head_dim_limit);\n    }\n    return false;\n  }\n  if (d_qk % 8 != 0 || d_v % 8 != 0) {\n    if (debug) {\n      TORCH_WARN(\"head_dim should be a multiple of 8\");\n    }\n    return false;\n  }\n  if (cudnn_version < 8906 && s_k % 64 != 0 ) {\n    if (debug) {\n      TORCH_WARN(\"not-multiple-of-64 seq_kv is not supported below 8.9.6\");\n    }\n    return false;\n  }\n  if (cudnn_version < 90000) {\n    if (s_q < 64) {\n      if (debug) {\n        TORCH_WARN(\"s_q less than 64 is not supported before cudnn 9.0.0\");\n      }\n      return false;\n    }\n    if (params.dropout != 0.0 && (s_q % 64 != 0 || s_k % 64 != 0)) {\n      if (debug) {\n        TORCH_WARN(\n            \"s_q not a multiple of 64 with padding/dropout is not supported with cudnn version 9.0.0\");\n      }\n      return false;\n    }\n  }\n  if (s_k == 1) {\n    if (debug) {\n      TORCH_WARN_ONCE(\"cudnn SDPA does not support key/value sequence length 1.\");\n    }\n    return false;\n  }\n  if (s_q == 1 && params.dropout != 0.0) {\n    if (debug) {\n      TORCH_WARN_ONCE(\"cudnn SDPA does not support query sequence length 1 with dropout.\");\n    }\n    return false;\n  }\n  return true;\n}\n\nbool check_cudnn_layout(sdp_params const& params, bool debug) {\n  const int64_t h = params.query.size(1);\n  const int64_t s_q = params.query.size(2);\n  const int64_t d = params.query.size(3);\n  const int64_t s_k = params.key.size(2);\n  const int64_t s_v = params.value.size(2);\n  // corresponds to cuDNN's \"packed QKV\" layout\n  const bool packed_query_layout_ok = (params.query.stride(0) == s_q * 3 * h * d) &&\n                                 (params.query.stride(1) == d) &&\n                                 (params.query.stride(2) == 3 * h * d) &&\n                                 (params.query.stride(3) == 1);\n  const bool packed_key_layout_ok = (params.key.stride(0) == s_k * 3 * h * d) &&\n                               (params.key.stride(1) == d) &&\n                               (params.key.stride(2) == 3 * h * d) &&\n                               (params.key.stride(3) == 1);\n  const bool packed_value_layout_ok = (params.value.stride(0) == s_v * 3 * h * d) &&\n                                 (params.value.stride(1) == d) &&\n                                 (params.value.stride(2) == 3 * h * d) &&\n                                 (params.value.stride(3) == 1);\n\n  const bool packed_layout_ok = packed_query_layout_ok && packed_key_layout_ok && packed_value_layout_ok;\n\n  const bool query_layout_ok = (params.query.stride(0) == s_q * h * d) &&\n                               (params.query.stride(1) == d) &&\n                               (params.query.stride(2) == h * d) &&\n                               (params.query.stride(3) == 1);\n  const bool key_layout_ok = (params.key.stride(0) == s_k * h * d) &&\n                              (params.key.stride(1) == d) &&\n                              (params.key.stride(2) == h * d) &&\n                              (params.key.stride(3) == 1);\n  const bool value_layout_ok = (params.value.stride(0) == s_v * h * d) &&\n                               (params.value.stride(1) == d) &&\n                               (params.value.stride(2) == h * d) &&\n                               (params.value.stride(3) == 1);\n\n  const bool layout_ok = query_layout_ok && key_layout_ok && value_layout_ok;\n\n  if (!packed_value_layout_ok && !layout_ok) {\n    if (debug) {\n      if (!packed_layout_ok) {\n        if (!packed_query_layout_ok) {\n          TORCH_WARN(\"Query tensor was not in cuDNN-supported packed QKV layout\", params.query.strides());\n        }\n        if (!packed_key_layout_ok) {\n          TORCH_WARN(\"Key tensor was not in cuDNN-supported packed QKV layout\", params.key.strides());\n        }\n        if (!packed_value_layout_ok) {\n          TORCH_WARN(\"Value tensor was not in cuDNN-supported packed QKV layout\", params.value.strides());\n        }\n      }\n      if (!layout_ok) {\n        if (!query_layout_ok) {\n          TORCH_WARN(\"Query tensor was not in cuDNN-supported unpacked QKV layout\", params.query.strides());\n        }\n        if (!key_layout_ok) {\n          TORCH_WARN(\"Key tensor was not in cuDNN-supported unpacked QKV layout\", params.key.strides());\n        }\n        if (!value_layout_ok) {\n          TORCH_WARN(\"Value tensor was not in cuDNN-supported unpacked QKV layout\", params.value.strides());\n        }\n      }\n    }\n    return false;\n  }\n  return true;\n}\n\nbool check_cudnn_hardware_support(sdp_params const& params, bool debug) {\n  using sm80 = SMVersion<8, 0>;\n  using sm121 = SMVersion<12, 1>;\n  auto dprops = at::cuda::getCurrentDeviceProperties();\n  if (!check_sm_version<sm80, sm121>(dprops)) {\n    if (debug) {\n      TORCH_WARN(\n          \"cuDNN MHA only supports gpu architectures in the range [sm80, sm121]. check_for_nested_inputs(sdp_params const& params, bool debug) {\n  static const bool enable_cudnn_nested = c10::utils::check_env(\"TORCH_CUDNN_SDPA_NESTED_TENSOR_ENABLED\") == true;\n  if (has_for_nested_inputs(params) && !enable_cudnn_nested) {\n    if (debug) {\n      TORCH_WARN(\"Experimental cuDNN SDPA nested tensor support is not enabled.\");\n    }\n    return false;\n  } else if !defined(CUDNN_VERSION)\n  if (debug) {\n    TORCH_WARN(\"Torch was not compiled with cuDNN attention.\");\n  }\n  return false;\n#endif\n#if defined(CUDNN_VERSION) && CUDNN_VERSION < 90000\n  if at::detail::getCUDAHooks().versionRuntimeCuDNN();\n  if (params.dropout > 0.0 && cudnn_version > 91100 && cudnn_version < 91400) {\n    if (debug) {\n      TORCH_WARN(CUDNN_VERSION, \" cuDNN version when we migrate to c++20\n  constexpr auto general_constraints =\n      c10::array_of<bool (*)(sdp_params const&, bool)>(\n          check_runtime_disabled_cudnn,\n          check_for_nested_inputs,\n          check_all_tensors_on_device,\n          check_tensor_shapes,\n          check_cudnn_deterministic,\n          check_dtypes_low_precision,\n          check_attn_mask_shape,\n          check_cudnn_hardware_support\n          );\n  for (auto& constraint : general_constraints) {\n    if (!constraint(params, debug)) {\n      return false;\n    }\n  }\n  constexpr auto dense_constraints =\n      c10::array_of<bool (*)(sdp_params const&, bool)>(\n      check_nonzero_sequence_lengths_dense,\n      check_last_dim_stride_equals_1_dense<true /*ignore_singleton_dim=*/>,\n      check_batch_size_and_num_heads_dense<true /*enable_gqa*/, false /*requires_same_num_heads*/>,\n      check_cudnn_tensor_shapes\n  );\n\n  if (has_only_dense_inputs(params)) {\n    for (auto& USE_FLASH_ATTENTION\n  return true;\n#else\n  return false;\n#endif\n}\n\nbool can_use_flash_attention(sdp_params const& params, bool debug) {\n#ifndef USE_FLASH_ATTENTION\n  if (debug) {\n    TORCH_WARN(\"Torch was not compiled with flash attention.\");\n  }\n  return false;\n#else // defined(USE_FLASH_ATTENTION)\n  // Define gate functions that determine if a flash kernel can be ran\n  // defined(USE_FLASH_ATTENTION)\n}\n\nbool can_use_mem_efficient_attention(sdp_params const& params, bool debug) {\n#ifndef USE_MEM_EFF_ATTENTION\n  TORCH_WARN_ONCE(!debug, \"Torch was not compiled with memory efficient attention.\");\n  return false;\n#endif\n  // Constraints specific to mem efficient attention\n  constexpr auto less_than_sm80_mem_efficient_dtypes =\n c10::array_of<at::ScalarType>(at::kHalf, at::kFloat, at::kBFloat16);\n#endif\n\n  //  Define gate functions that determine if a mem efficient kernel can be ran\n  constexpr auto general_constraints =      check_batch_size_and_num_heads_dense<false /*supports_grouped_query_attention=*/>);\n    for (auto& constraint : dense_constraints) {\n      if (!constraint(params, debug)) {\n        return false;\n      }\n    }\n  }\n\n#ifdef USE_ROCM\n  if (params.attn_mask.has_value()) {\n    const auto q_dtype = params.query.dtype();\n    const auto bias_dtype = params.attn_mask.value().dtype();\n greater_than_or_equal_sm80_mem_efficient_dtypes, debug);\n  }\n#endif\n  return check_tensor_dtype(params, less_than_sm80_mem_efficient_dtypes, debug);\n}\n\nSDPBackend select_sdp_backend(sdp_params const& kernel_params) {\n  // This function defines the priority order of the different sdp backends\n  // 1. Flash Attention\n  // 2. Mem Efficient Attention\n  // 3. Math fallback\n  auto& ctx = at::globalContext();\n  if (!ctx.userEnabledMathSDP() && !ctx.userEnabledFlashSDP() &&\n      !ctx.userEnabledMemEfficientSDP() && !ctx.userEnabledCuDNNSDP()) {\n    return SDPBackend::error;\n  }\n  // Get ideal kernel ordering\n  const auto ordering = priority_order(kernel_params);\n\n  // Because TORCHCHECK checks if condition is true we negate debug so that\n  // The statements will be printed when debug is true\n  bool print_debug = false;\n  for (auto& backend : ordering) {\n    switch (backend) {\n      case SDPBackend::cudnn_attention:\n        if (sdp::can_use_cudnn_attention(kernel_params, print_debug)) {\n              return SDPBackend::cudnn_attention;\n        }\n        break;\n      case SDPBackend::flash_attention:\n        if (sdp::can_use_flash_attention(kernel_params, print_debug)) {\n          return SDPBackend::flash_attention;\n        }\n        break;\n      case SDPBackend::efficient_attention:\n        if (sdp::can_use_mem_efficient_attention(kernel_params, print_debug)) {\n          return SDPBackend::efficient_attention;\n        }\n        break;\n      case SDPBackend::math:\n        if (ctx.userEnabledMathSDP()) {\n          return SDPBackend::math;\n        }\n        break;\n      case SDPBackend::overrideable:\n        if (ctx.userEnabledOverrideableSDP()) {\n          TORCH_CHECK(false, \"Invalid backend\");\n        }\n        break;\n      default:\n        TORCH_CHECK(false, \"Invalid backend\");\n    }\n  }\n  // If we have gotten to this point then two things have happened:\n  // 1. use_flash_attention or use_mem_efficient did not satisfy the\n  // constraints to be ran\n  // 2. The user has explicitly disabled the math kernel\n  // We then re-run the kernel checks with debug enabled to print out the\n  // reason why the kernel was not selected\n\n  print_debug = true;\n  TORCH_WARN(\"Memory efficient kernel not used because:\");\n  sdp::can_use_mem_efficient_attention(kernel_params, print_debug);\n  TORCH_WARN(\"Flash attention kernel not used because:\");\n  sdp::can_use_flash_attention(kernel_params, print_debug);\n  TORCH_WARN(\"cuDNN attention kernel not used because:\");\n  sdp::can_use_cudnn_attention(kernel_params, print_debug);\n  TORCH_CHECK(!print_debug, \"No available kernel. bool is_causal,\n    float dropout_probability,\n    const Tensor& q,\n    const Tensor& k,\n    const Tensor& v,\n    const std::optional<Tensor>& attn_bias,\n    const Tensor& o,\n    const Tensor& dO,\n    const Tensor& softmaxstats,\n    Tensor& dQ,\n    Tensor& dK,\n    Tensor& dV,\n    const Tensor& dropoutseed,\n    const Tensor& dropoutoffset) {\n  TORCH_CHECK(\n      false, \"PyTorch was not compiled with cuDNN Flash Attention enabled!\");\n}\n\nvoid run_cudnn_SDP_bprop_nestedtensor(\n    int64_t b,\n    int64_t h_q,\n    int64_t h_k,\n    int64_t h_v,\n    int64_t s_q,\n    int64_t s_kv,\n    int64_t d_qk,\n    int64_t d_v,\n\n    float scaling_factor,\n    bool is_causal,\n    float dropout_probability,\n    const Tensor& cum_seqlen_q,\n    const Tensor& cum_seqlen_kv,\n    const Tensor& q,\n    const Tensor& k,\n    const Tensor& v,\n    const std::optional<Tensor>& attn_bias,\n    const Tensor& o,\n    const Tensor& dO,\n    const Tensor& softmaxstats,\n    Tensor& dQ,\n    Tensor& dK,\n    Tensor& dV,\n    const Tensor& dropoutseed,\n    const Tensor& dropoutoffset) {\n  TORCH_CHECK(\n      false, \"PyTorch was not compiled with cuDNN Flash Attention enabled!\");\n}\n\n} // namespace native\n} // namespace at\n\n#else // AT_CUDNN_ENABLED && defined(CUDNN_VERSION) && CUDNN_VERSION >= 8900\n#include <ATen/cudnn/Descriptors.h>\n#include <ATen/cudnn/Types.h>\n#include <ATen/cudnn/Utils.h>\n#include <ATen/native/cudnn/MHA.h>\n#include <ATen/native/transformers/sdp_utils.h>\n\n#include <ATen/cuda/Exceptions.h>\n\n#include <ATen/TensorUtils.h>\n#include <ATen/native/utils/ParamsHash.h>\n\n#include <c10/cuda/CUDACachingAllocator.h>\n#include <cudnn.h>\n\n#include <iostream>\n\nnamespace at {\nnamespace native {\n\n#include <cudnn_frontend.h>\n\nnamespace fe = cudnn_frontend;\n\nconstexpr uint8_t MAX_MHA_DIM = 4;\n\n// Whether we will use ragged offsets in the dense (non-nested) path\n// to avoid recompilation\nbool use_ragged_in_dense(\n    const Tensor& q,\n    const Tensor& k,\n    const Tensor& v,\n    const Tensor& o,\n    bool has_bias) {\n  static bool flag =\n      c10::utils::check_env(\"TORCH_CUDNN_SDPA_AVOID_RECOMPILE\") == true;\n  if (!flag) {\n    return flag;\n  }\n  TORCH_WARN_ONCE(\n      \"TORCH_CUDNN_SDPA_AVOID_RECOMPILE=1 is currently experimental. \"\n      \"Please report any issues to https://github.com/pytorch/pytorch/issues.\");\n  if (has_bias) {\n    TORCH_WARN_ONCE(\n        \"TORCH_CUDNN_SDPA_AVOID_RECOMPILE=1 only works without bias.\"\n        \"Consider using the is_causal hint instead of bias for causal masking.\"\n        \"Falling back to regular dense case, which may trigger excessive recompilation.\");\n    return !has_bias;\n  }\n  bool all_bshd = q.dim() == 4 && q.transpose(1, 2).is_contiguous() &&\n      k.dim() == 4 && k.transpose(1, 2).is_contiguous() && v.dim() == 4 &&\n      v.transpose(1, 2).is_contiguous() && o.dim() == 4 &&\n      o.transpose(1, 2).is_contiguous();\n  if (!all_bshd) {\n    TORCH_WARN_ONCE(\n        \"TORCH_CUDNN_SDPA_AVOID_RECOMPILE=1 only works with Q, K, V, and output in BSHD memory layout,\"\n        \"e.g., Q, K, V must be allocated with torch.randn((B, S, H, D).transpose(1, 2).\"\n        \"Falling back to regualr dense case, which may trigger excessive recompilation.\");\n  }\n  return all_bshd;\n}\n\nint roundup_power2(int dim) {\n  if (!dim) {\n    return 1;\n  }\n  dim--;\n  dim |= dim >> 1;\n  dim |= dim >> 2;\n  dim |= dim >> 4;\n  dim |= dim >> 8;\n  dim |= dim >> 16;\n  dim++;\n  return dim;\n}\n\nstruct MHAParams {\n  c10::DeviceIndex device_id;\n  fe::DataType_t dataType;\n  std::array<int, MAX_MHA_DIM> q_dim;\n  std::array<int, MAX_MHA_DIM> k_dim;\n  std::array<int, MAX_MHA_DIM> v_dim;\n  std::array<int, MAX_MHA_DIM> q_stride;\n  std::array<int, MAX_MHA_DIM> k_stride;\n  std::array<int, MAX_MHA_DIM> v_stride;\n  std::array<int, MAX_MHA_DIM> bias_dim;\n  std::array<int, MAX_MHA_DIM> bias_stride;\n  int64_t b;\n  int64_t h;\n  int64_t s_q;\n  int64_t s_kv;\n  int64_t d_qk;\n  int64_t d_v;\n  double dropout_probability;\n  bool is_causal;\n  bool return_softmaxstats;\n  // might be redundant if we take 0 dim/stride\n  // as signaling no-bias\n  bool has_attn_bias;\n  bool use_ragged;\n};\n\nvoid setMHAParams(\n    MHAParams& params,\n    int64_t b,\n    int64_t h,\n    int64_t s_q,\n    int64_t s_kv,\n    int64_t d_qk,\n    int64_t d_v,\n    const Tensor& q,\n    const Tensor& k,\n    const Tensor& v,\n    const std::optional<Tensor>& attn_bias,\n    double dropout_probability,\n    bool is_causal,\n    bool return_softmaxstats,\n    bool is_nested) {\n  memset(&params, 0, sizeof(MHAParams));\n  params.device_id = at::cuda::current_device();\n  params.dataType = fe::DataType_t::HALF;\n  if (q.scalar_type() == kBFloat16) {\n    params.dataType = fe::DataType_t::BFLOAT16;\n  }\n  params.b = b;\n  params.h = h;\n  params.d_qk = d_qk;\n  params.d_v = d_v;\n  params.s_q = s_q;\n  params.s_kv = s_kv;\n  params.dropout_probability = dropout_probability;\n  params.is_causal = is_causal;\n  params.return_softmaxstats = return_softmaxstats;\n  params.has_attn_bias = attn_bias.has_value();\n  // Expect 4D dense tensor, 3D nested case (THD)\n  TORCH_INTERNAL_ASSERT(\n      q.sizes().size() == (uint8_t)(MAX_MHA_DIM - (uint8_t)is_nested),\n      \"Q tensor has unexpected number of dims, please report a bug to PyTorch.\");\n  TORCH_INTERNAL_ASSERT(\n      q.strides().size() == (uint8_t)(MAX_MHA_DIM - (uint8_t)is_nested),\n      \"Q tensor has unexpected number of dims, please report a bug to PyTorch.\");\n  TORCH_INTERNAL_ASSERT(\n      k.sizes().size() == (uint8_t)(MAX_MHA_DIM - (uint8_t)is_nested),\n      \"K tensor has unexpected number of dims, please report a bug to PyTorch.\");\n  TORCH_INTERNAL_ASSERT(\n      k.strides().size() == (uint8_t)(MAX_MHA_DIM - (uint8_t)is_nested),\n      \"K tensor has unexpected number of dims, please report a bug to PyTorch.\");\n  TORCH_INTERNAL_ASSERT(\n      v.sizes().size() == (uint8_t)(MAX_MHA_DIM - (uint8_t)is_nested),\n      \"V tensor has unexpected number of dims, please report a bug to PyTorch.\");\n  TORCH_INTERNAL_ASSERT(\n      v.strides().size() == (uint8_t)(MAX_MHA_DIM - (uint8_t)is_nested),\n      \"V tensor has unexpected number of dims, please report a bug to PyTorch.\");\n  std::copy(q.sizes().begin(), q.sizes().end(), params.q_dim.begin());\n  std::copy(q.strides().begin(), q.strides().end(), params.q_stride.begin());\n  std::copy(k.sizes().begin(), k.sizes().end(), params.k_dim.begin());\n  std::copy(k.strides().begin(), k.strides().end(), params.k_stride.begin());\n  std::copy(v.sizes().begin(), v.sizes().end(), params.v_dim.begin());\n  std::copy(v.strides().begin(), v.strides().end(), params.v_stride.begin());\n  bool use_ragged = use_ragged_in_dense(q, k, v, q, params.has_attn_bias);\n  params.use_ragged = use_ragged;\n  if (use_ragged) {\n    // ignore B - stride in BSHD (THD) avoid-recompile\n    params.q_stride[0] = INT_MAX;\n    params.k_stride[0] = INT_MAX;\n    params.v_stride[0] = INT_MAX;\n    // fix seqlen to rounded value\n    params.s_q = roundup_power2(params.s_q);\n    params.s_kv = roundup_power2(params.s_kv);\n    params.q_dim[2] = roundup_power2(params.q_dim[2]);\n    params.k_dim[2] = roundup_power2(params.k_dim[2]);\n    params.v_dim[2] = roundup_power2(params.v_dim[2]);\n  }\n  // uninit is OK as the struct is memset 0'd\n  if (params.has_attn_bias) {\n    std::copy(\n        attn_bias.value().sizes().begin(),\n        attn_bias.value().sizes().end(),\n        params.bias_dim.begin());\n    std::copy(\n        attn_bias.value().strides().begin(),\n        attn_bias.value().strides().end(),\n        params.bias_stride.begin());\n  }\n}\n\nstruct MHACacheKeyWrapper : ParamsWrapper<MHAParams> {\n  MHACacheKeyWrapper(\n      int64_t b,\n      int64_t h,\n      int64_t s_q,\n      int64_t s_kv,\n      int64_t d_qk,\n      int64_t d_v,\n      const Tensor& q,\n      const Tensor& k,\n      const Tensor& v,\n      const std::optional<Tensor>& attn_bias,\n      double dropout_probability,\n      bool is_causal,\n      bool return_softmaxstats,\n      bool is_nested) {\n    setMHAParams(\n        this->pod,\n        b,\n        h,\n        s_q,\n        s_kv,\n        d_qk,\n        d_v,\n        q,\n        k,\n        v,\n        attn_bias,\n        dropout_probability,\n        is_causal,\n        return_softmaxstats,\n        is_nested);\n  }\n};\n\ntemplate <typename T, typename KeyType>\nstruct MHAGraphCache {\n  std::unordered_map<KeyType, T, ParamsWrapperHash<KeyType>> engine_cache;\n  int count = 0;\n  int hits = 0;\n\n  // no mutexes here as caches are now thread local for v8, can also return a\n  // pointer to the Execution Plan if we know it will not be invalidated by\n  // another thread\n  T* find(const KeyType& key) {\n    static bool flag =\n        c10::utils::check_env(\"TORCH_CUDNN_SDPA_CACHE_DEBUG\") == true;\n    if (flag && count) {\n      TORCH_WARN(\n          \"SDPA Cache Called \",\n          count,\n          \" times. Hit rate: \",\n          100 * hits / count,\n          \"%\");\n    }\n    count++;\n    auto it = engine_cache.find(key);\n    if (it == engine_cache.end()) {\n      return nullptr;\n    }\n    hits++;\n    return &(it->second);\n  }\n\n  void update(const KeyType& key, T& results) {\n    engine_cache.erase(key);\n    engine_cache.emplace(key, std::move(results));\n  }\n};\n\n// @eqy: use thread local caches as cuDNN Execution Plans are not guaranteed to\n// be thread safe across all engines see Limitations in\n// https://docs.nvidia.com/deeplearning/cudnn/backend/latest/release-notes.html\n// We also leak the caches to workaround potential teardown race issues.\n\nauto& getMHAGraphCache_() {\n  thread_local auto& instance =\n      *new MHAGraphCache<std::shared_ptr<fe::graph::Graph>, MHACacheKeyWrapper>;\n  return instance;\n}\n\nauto& getMHAGraphBackwardCache_() {\n  thread_local auto& instance =\n      *new MHAGraphCache<std::shared_ptr<fe::graph::Graph>, MHACacheKeyWrapper>;\n  return instance;\n}\n\nnamespace {\n\nenum UIDS {\n  Q,\n  K,\n  V,\n  O,\n  BIAS,\n  SCALE,\n  SEED,\n  OFFSET,\n  LSE,\n  DO,\n  DQ,\n  DK,\n  DV,\n  SEQ_LEN_Q,\n  SEQ_LEN_KV,\n  RAG_Q_OFF,\n  RAG_K_OFF,\n  RAG_V_OFF,\n  RAG_O_OFF,\n  RAG_LSE_OFF\n};\n\n// analogous to the same function in Descriptors.h for cuDNN Convolutions...\nauto fixSizeOneDimStrideSDPA(\n    const IntArrayRef sizes,\n    std::vector<int64_t> strides) {\n  int dims = sizes.size();\n  for (int d = 0; d < dims; d++) {\n    int64_t curr_stride = strides[d];\n    if (sizes[d] == 1 && !curr_stride) {\n      curr_stride = 1;\n      for (int d2 = d + 1; d2 < dims; d2++) {\n        curr_stride *= strides[d2];\n      }\n      strides[d] = curr_stride;\n    }\n  }\n  return strides;\n}\n\n} // namespace\n\nauto build_graph(\n    int64_t b,\n    int64_t h,\n    int64_t s_q,\n    int64_t s_kv,\n    int64_t d_qk,\n    int64_t d_v,\n    float scaling_factor,\n    bool return_softmaxstats,\n    bool is_causal,\n    double dropout_probability,\n    const Tensor& q,\n    const Tensor& k,\n    const Tensor& v,\n    const std::optional<Tensor>& attn_bias,\n    Tensor& softmaxstats,\n    Tensor& o,\n    Tensor& dropoutseed,\n    Tensor& dropoutoffset,\n    cudnnHandle_t& handle) {\n  auto dtype = fe::DataType_t::HALF;\n  if (q.scalar_type() == kBFloat16) {\n    dtype = fe::DataType_t::BFLOAT16;\n  }\n  auto mha_graph = std::make_shared<fe::graph::Graph>();\n  // We're baking in float accumulation and scale types\n  // in theory the graph may support other types, but they\n  // have not been tested\n  mha_graph->set_io_data_type(dtype)\n      .set_intermediate_data_type(fe::DataType_t::FLOAT)\n      .set_compute_data_type(fe::DataType_t::FLOAT);\n  auto attn_scale =\n      mha_graph->tensor(fe::graph::Tensor_attributes()\n                            .set_uid(SCALE)\n                            .set_name(\"Attn_scale\")\n                            .set_dim({1, 1, 1, 1})\n                            .set_stride({1, 1, 1, 1})\n                            .set_is_pass_by_value(true)\n                            .set_data_type(fe::DataType_t::FLOAT));\n  auto scaled_dot_product_flash_attention_options =\n      fe::graph::SDPA_attributes()\n          .set_name(\"CUDNN_SDPA\")\n          .set_is_inference(return_softmaxstats == false)\n          // TODO(eqy): switch to this API once cuDNN FE is upgraded\n          // .set_generate_stats(return_softmaxstats)\n          .set_causal_mask(is_causal)\n          .set_attn_scale(attn_scale);\n  if (use_ragged_in_dense(q, k, v, o, attn_bias.has_value())) {\n    auto SEQ_LEN_Q_ =\n        mha_graph->tensor(fe::graph::Tensor_attributes()\n                              .set_uid(SEQ_LEN_Q)\n                              .set_name(\"Seq_q\")\n                              .set_dim({b, 1, 1, 1})\n                              .set_stride({1, 1, 1, 1})\n                              .set_data_type(fe::DataType_t::INT32));\n    auto SEQ_LEN_KV_ =\n        mha_graph->tensor(fe::graph::Tensor_attributes()\n                              .set_uid(SEQ_LEN_KV)\n                              .set_name(\"Seq_kv\")\n                              .set_dim({b, 1, 1, 1})\n                              .set_stride({1, 1, 1, 1})\n                              .set_data_type(fe::DataType_t::INT32));\n    scaled_dot_product_flash_attention_options.set_seq_len_q(SEQ_LEN_Q_)\n        .set_seq_len_kv(SEQ_LEN_KV_)\n        .set_padding_mask(true);\n  }\n  if (dropout_probability != 0.0f) {\n    auto seed = mha_graph->tensor(fe::graph::Tensor_attributes()\n                                      .set_uid(SEED)\n                                      .set_name(\"Seed\")\n                                      .set_dim({1, 1, 1, 1})\n                                      .set_stride({1, 1, 1, 1})\n                                      .set_data_type(\n                                          dropoutseed.dtype() == kInt\n                                              ? fe::DataType_t::INT32\n                                              : fe::DataType_t::INT64));\n    auto offset = mha_graph->tensor(fe::graph::Tensor_attributes()\n                                        .set_uid(OFFSET)\n                                        .set_name(\"Offset\")\n                                        .set_dim({1, 1, 1, 1})\n                                        .set_stride({1, 1, 1, 1})\n                                        .set_data_type(\n                                            dropoutoffset.dtype() == kInt\n                                                ? fe::DataType_t::INT32\n                                                : fe::DataType_t::INT64));\n    scaled_dot_product_flash_attention_options.set_dropout(\n        dropout_probability, seed, offset);\n  }\n  auto Q_ = mha_graph->tensor(\n      fe::graph::Tensor_attributes().set_uid(Q).set_name(\"Q\"));\n  auto K_ = mha_graph->tensor(\n      fe::graph::Tensor_attributes().set_uid(K).set_name(\"K\"));\n  auto V_ = mha_graph->tensor(\n      fe::graph::Tensor_attributes().set_uid(V).set_name(\"V\"));\n  std::optional<std::shared_ptr<fe::graph::Tensor_attributes>> bias;\n  if (attn_bias.has_value()) {\n    bias =\n        mha_graph->tensor(fe::graph::Tensor_attributes()\n                              .set_uid(BIAS)\n                              .set_name(\"bias\")\n                              .set_dim(attn_bias.value().sizes().vec())\n                              .set_stride(attn_bias.value().strides().vec()));\n    scaled_dot_product_flash_attention_options.set_bias(bias.value());\n  }\n\n  auto [O_, Stats] =\n      mha_graph->sdpa(Q_, K_, V_, scaled_dot_product_flash_attention_options);\n  O_->set_uid(O).set_output(true);\n  if (Stats) {\n    Stats->set_uid(LSE)\n        .set_output(true)\n        .set_data_type(fe::DataType_t::FLOAT)\n        .set_stride(softmaxstats.strides().vec());\n  }\n  if (use_ragged_in_dense(q, k, v, o, attn_bias.has_value())) {\n    auto RAG_Q_OFF_ =\n        mha_graph->tensor(fe::graph::Tensor_attributes()\n                              .set_uid(RAG_Q_OFF)\n                              .set_name(\"cum_seq_q\")\n                              .set_dim({b + 1, 1, 1, 1})\n                              .set_stride({1, 1, 1, 1})\n                              .set_data_type(fe::DataType_t::INT32));\n    auto RAG_K_OFF_ =\n        mha_graph->tensor(fe::graph::Tensor_attributes()\n                              .set_uid(RAG_K_OFF)\n                              .set_name(\"cum_seq_k\")\n                              .set_dim({b + 1, 1, 1, 1})\n                              .set_stride({1, 1, 1, 1})\n                              .set_data_type(fe::DataType_t::INT32));\n    auto RAG_V_OFF_ =\n        mha_graph->tensor(fe::graph::Tensor_attributes()\n                              .set_uid(RAG_V_OFF)\n                              .set_name(\"cum_seq_v\")\n                              .set_dim({b + 1, 1, 1, 1})\n                              .set_stride({1, 1, 1, 1})\n                              .set_data_type(fe::DataType_t::INT32));\n    auto RAG_O_OFF_ =\n        mha_graph->tensor(fe::graph::Tensor_attributes()\n                              .set_uid(RAG_O_OFF)\n                              .set_name(\"cum_seq_o\")\n                              .set_dim({b + 1, 1, 1, 1})\n                              .set_stride({1, 1, 1, 1})\n                              .set_data_type(fe::DataType_t::INT32));\n    auto RAG_STATS_OFF_ =\n        mha_graph->tensor(fe::graph::Tensor_attributes()\n                              .set_uid(RAG_LSE_OFF)\n                              .set_name(\"cum_seq_stats\")\n                              .set_dim({b + 1, 1, 1, 1})\n                              .set_stride({1, 1, 1, 1})\n                              .set_data_type(fe::DataType_t::INT32));\n    O_->set_ragged_offset(RAG_O_OFF_);\n    Q_->set_ragged_offset(RAG_Q_OFF_);\n    K_->set_ragged_offset(RAG_K_OFF_);\n    V_->set_ragged_offset(RAG_V_OFF_);\n    auto qsizevec = q.sizes().vec();\n    auto ksizevec = k.sizes().vec();\n    auto vsizevec = v.sizes().vec();\n    auto osizevec = o.sizes().vec();\n    qsizevec[2] = roundup_power2(qsizevec[2]);\n    ksizevec[2] = roundup_power2(ksizevec[2]);\n    vsizevec[2] = roundup_power2(vsizevec[2]);\n    osizevec[2] = roundup_power2(osizevec[2]);\n    // we checked for BSHD contig., set fake strides as cuDNN will complain\n    // if e.g., a ragged dim is smaller than a non-ragged one:\n    // consider HBSD tensor where H is 1\n    Q_->set_dim(qsizevec).set_stride(\n        {INT_MAX, qsizevec[3], qsizevec[1] * qsizevec[3], 1});\n    K_->set_dim(ksizevec).set_stride(\n        {INT_MAX, ksizevec[3], ksizevec[1] * ksizevec[3], 1});\n    V_->set_dim(vsizevec).set_stride(\n        {INT_MAX, vsizevec[3], vsizevec[1] * vsizevec[3], 1});\n    O_->set_dim(osizevec).set_stride(\n        {INT_MAX, osizevec[3], osizevec[1] * osizevec[3], 1});\n    if (Stats) {\n      Stats->set_ragged_offset(RAG_STATS_OFF_);\n      auto statssizevec = softmaxstats.sizes().vec();\n      statssizevec[2] = roundup_power2(statssizevec[2]);\n      Stats->set_dim(statssizevec);\n    }\n  } else {\n    Q_->set_dim(q.sizes().vec())\n        .set_stride(fixSizeOneDimStrideSDPA(q.sizes(), q.strides().vec()));\n    K_->set_dim(k.sizes().vec())\n        .set_stride(fixSizeOneDimStrideSDPA(k.sizes(), k.strides().vec()));\n    V_->set_dim(v.sizes().vec())\n        .set_stride(fixSizeOneDimStrideSDPA(v.sizes(), v.strides().vec()));\n    O_->set_dim(o.sizes().vec())\n        .set_stride(fixSizeOneDimStrideSDPA(o.sizes(), o.strides().vec()));\n    if (Stats) {\n      Stats->set_dim(softmaxstats.sizes().vec());\n    }\n  }\n\n  AT_CUDNN_FRONTEND_CHECK(mha_graph->validate());\n  AT_CUDNN_FRONTEND_CHECK(mha_graph->build_operation_graph(handle));\n  AT_CUDNN_FRONTEND_CHECK(\n      mha_graph->create_execution_plans({fe::HeurMode_t::A}));\n  AT_CUDNN_FRONTEND_CHECK(mha_graph->check_support(handle));\n  AT_CUDNN_FRONTEND_CHECK(mha_graph->build_plans(handle));\n\n  return mha_graph;\n}\n\nauto build_graph_nestedtensor(\n    int64_t b,\n is_causal,\n    double dropout_probability,\n    const Tensor& cum_seqlen_q,\n    const Tensor& cum_seqlen_kv,\n    const Tensor& q,\n    const Tensor& k,\n    const Tensor& v,\n    const std::optional<Tensor>& attn_bias,\n    Tensor& softmaxstats,\n    Tensor& o,\n    Tensor& dropoutseed,\n    Tensor& dropoutoffset,\n    cudnnHandle_t& handle) {\n  auto dtype = fe::DataType_t::HALF;\n  if (q.scalar_type() == kBFloat16) {\n    dtype = fe::DataType_t::BFLOAT16;\n  }\n  auto mha_graph = std::make_shared<fe::graph::Graph>();\n  // We're baking in float accumulation and scale types\n  // in theory the graph may support other types, but they\n  // have not been tested\n  mha_graph->set_io_data_type(dtype)\n      .set_intermediate_data_type(fe::DataType_t::FLOAT)\n      .set_compute_data_type(fe::DataType_t::FLOAT);\n  auto attn_scale =\n      mha_graph->tensor(fe::graph::Tensor_attributes()\n                            .set_uid(SCALE)\n                            .set_name(\"Attn_scale\")\n                            .set_dim({1, 1, 1, 1})\n                            .set_stride({1, 1, 1, 1})\n                            .set_is_pass_by_value(true)\n                            .set_data_type(fe::DataType_t::FLOAT));\n  auto SEQ_LEN_Q_ =\n      mha_graph->tensor(fe::graph::Tensor_attributes()\n                            .set_uid(SEQ_LEN_Q)\n                            .set_name(\"Seq_q\")\n                            .set_dim({b, 1, 1, 1})\n                            .set_stride({1, 1, 1, 1})\n                            .set_data_type(fe::DataType_t::INT32));\n  auto SEQ_LEN_KV_ =\n      mha_graph->tensor(fe::graph::Tensor_attributes()\n                            .set_uid(SEQ_LEN_KV)\n                            .set_name(\"Seq_kv\")\n                            .set_dim({b, 1, 1, 1})\n                            .set_stride({1, 1, 1, 1})\n                            .set_data_type(fe::DataType_t::INT32));\n\n  auto scaled_dot_product_flash_attention_options =\n      fe::graph::SDPA_attributes()\n          .set_name(\"CUDNN_SDPA_NESTEDTENSOR\")\n          .set_is_inference(return_softmaxstats == false)\n          // TODO(eqy): switch to this API once cuDNN FE is upgraded\n          // .set_generate_stats(return_softmaxstats)\n          .set_causal_mask(is_causal)\n          .set_attn_scale(attn_scale)\n          .set_seq_len_q(SEQ_LEN_Q_)\n          .set_seq_len_kv(SEQ_LEN_KV_)\n          .set_padding_mask(true);\n  if (dropout_probability != 0.0f) {\n    auto seed = mha_graph->tensor(fe::graph::Tensor_attributes()\n                                      .set_uid(SEED)\n                                      .set_name(\"Seed\")\n                                      .set_dim({1, 1, 1, 1})\n                                      .set_stride({1, 1, 1, 1})\n                                      .set_data_type(\n                                          dropoutseed.dtype() == kInt\n                                              ? fe::DataType_t::INT32\n                                              : fe::DataType_t::INT64));\n    auto offset = mha_graph->tensor(fe::graph::Tensor_attributes()\n                                        .set_uid(OFFSET)\n                                        .set_name(\"Offset\")\n                                        .set_dim({1, 1, 1, 1})\n                                        .set_stride({1, 1, 1, 1})\n                                        .set_data_type(\n                                            dropoutoffset.dtype() == kInt\n                                                ? fe::DataType_t::INT32\n                                                : fe::DataType_t::INT64));\n    scaled_dot_product_flash_attention_options.set_dropout(\n        dropout_probability, seed, offset);\n  }\n  // We hardcode BSHD to cuDNN even though the underlying layout is THD\n  auto q_strides = q.strides();\n  auto k_strides = k.strides();\n  auto v_strides = v.strides();\n  // NB: cuDNN API shape is transposed: we pass it nominally as HTD\n  constexpr int strideidx0 = 1;\n  constexpr int strideidx1 = 0;\n  constexpr int strideidx2 = 2;\n  auto Q_ = mha_graph->tensor(fe::graph::Tensor_attributes()\n                                  .set_uid(Q)\n                                  .set_name(\"Q\")\n                                  .set_dim({b, h_q, s_q, d_qk})\n                                  .set_stride(\n                                      {INT_MAX,\n                                       q_strides[strideidx0],\n                                       q_strides[strideidx1],\n                                       q_strides[strideidx2]}));\n  auto K_ = mha_graph->tensor(fe::graph::Tensor_attributes()\n                                  .set_uid(K)\n                                  .set_name(\"K\")\n                                  .set_dim({b, h_k, s_kv, d_qk})\n                                  .set_stride(\n                                      {INT_MAX,\n                                       k_strides[strideidx0],\n                                       k_strides[strideidx1],\n                                       k_strides[strideidx2]}));\n  auto V_ = mha_graph->tensor(fe::graph::Tensor_attributes()\n                                  .set_uid(V)\n                                  .set_name(\"V\")\n                                  .set_dim({b, h_v, s_kv, d_v})\n                                  .set_stride(\n                                      {INT_MAX,\n                                       v_strides[strideidx0],\n                                       v_strides[strideidx1],\n                                       v_strides[strideidx2]}));\n  std::optional<std::shared_ptr<fe::graph::Tensor_attributes>> bias;\n  if (attn_bias.has_value()) {\n    TORCH_CHECK(\n        false,\n        \"attn_bias not yet supportd with cuDNN Attention and NestedTensor\");\n    bias =\n        mha_graph->tensor(fe::graph::Tensor_attributes()\n                              .set_uid(BIAS)\n                              .set_name(\"bias\")\n                              .set_dim(attn_bias.value().sizes().vec())\n                              .set_stride(attn_bias.value().strides().vec()));\n    scaled_dot_product_flash_attention_options.set_bias(bias.value());\n  }\n  auto RAG_Q_OFF_ =\n      mha_graph->tensor(fe::graph::Tensor_attributes()\n                            .set_uid(RAG_Q_OFF)\n                            .set_name(\"cum_seq_q\")\n                            .set_dim({b + 1, 1, 1, 1})\n                            .set_stride({1, 1, 1, 1})\n                            .set_data_type(fe::DataType_t::INT32));\n  auto RAG_K_OFF_ =\n      mha_graph->tensor(fe::graph::Tensor_attributes()\n                            .set_uid(RAG_K_OFF)\n                            .set_name(\"cum_seq_k\")\n                            .set_dim({b + 1, 1, 1, 1})\n                            .set_stride({1, 1, 1, 1})\n                            .set_data_type(fe::DataType_t::INT32));\n  auto RAG_V_OFF_ =\n      mha_graph->tensor(fe::graph::Tensor_attributes()\n                            .set_uid(RAG_V_OFF)\n                            .set_name(\"cum_seq_v\")\n                            .set_dim({b + 1, 1, 1, 1})\n                            .set_stride({1, 1, 1, 1})\n                            .set_data_type(fe::DataType_t::INT32));\n  auto RAG_O_OFF_ =\n      mha_graph->tensor(fe::graph::Tensor_attributes()\n                            .set_uid(RAG_O_OFF)\n                            .set_name(\"cum_seq_o\")\n                            .set_dim({b + 1, 1, 1, 1})\n                            .set_stride({1, 1, 1, 1})\n                            .set_data_type(fe::DataType_t::INT32));\n  Q_->set_ragged_offset(RAG_Q_OFF_);\n  K_->set_ragged_offset(RAG_K_OFF_);\n  V_->set_ragged_offset(RAG_V_OFF_);\n  auto [O_, Stats] =\n      mha_graph->sdpa(Q_, K_, V_, scaled_dot_product_flash_attention_options);\n  auto o_strides = o.strides();\n  O_->set_output(true)\n      .set_uid(O)\n      .set_dim({b, h_q, s_q, d_v})\n      .set_stride(\n          {INT_MAX,\n           o_strides[strideidx0],\n           o_strides[strideidx1],\n           o_strides[strideidx2]});\n\n  O_->set_ragged_offset(RAG_O_OFF_);\n  if (Stats) {\n    auto RAG_STATS_OFF =\n        mha_graph->tensor(fe::graph::Tensor_attributes()\n                              .set_uid(RAG_LSE_OFF)\n                              .set_name(\"cum_seq_stats\")\n                              .set_dim({b + 1, 1, 1, 1})\n                              .set_stride({1, 1, 1, 1})\n                              .set_data_type(fe::DataType_t::INT32));\n    Stats->set_output(true)\n        .set_uid(LSE)\n        .set_data_type(fe::DataType_t::FLOAT)\n        .set_dim({b, h_q, s_q, 1})\n        .set_stride({h_q * s_q, 1, h_q, 1});\n    Stats->set_ragged_offset(RAG_STATS_OFF);\n  }\n  AT_CUDNN_FRONTEND_CHECK(mha_graph->validate());\n  AT_CUDNN_FRONTEND_CHECK(mha_graph->build_operation_graph(handle));\n  AT_CUDNN_FRONTEND_CHECK(\n      mha_graph->create_execution_plans({fe::HeurMode_t::A}));\n  AT_CUDNN_FRONTEND_CHECK(mha_graph->check_support(handle));\n  AT_CUDNN_FRONTEND_CHECK(mha_graph->build_plans(handle));\n  return mha_graph;\n}\n\nauto build_graph_backward(\n    int64_t b,\n    int64_t h,\n    int64_t s_q,\n    int64_t s_kv,\n    int64_t d_qk,\n    int64_t d_v,\n    float scaling_factor,\n    bool is_causal,\n    float dropout_probability,\n    const Tensor& q,\n    const Tensor& k,\n    const Tensor& v,\n    const std::optional<Tensor>& attn_bias,\n    const Tensor& o,\n    const Tensor& dO,\n    const Tensor& softmaxstats,\n    Tensor& dQ,\n    Tensor& dK,\n    Tensor& dV,\n    const Tensor& dropoutseed,\n    const Tensor& dropoutoffset,\n    cudnnHandle_t& handle) {\n  auto dtype = fe::DataType_t::HALF;\n  if (q.scalar_type() == kBFloat16) {\n    dtype = fe::DataType_t::BFLOAT16;\n  }\n  auto mha_graph = std::make_shared<fe::graph::Graph>();\n  // We're baking in float accumulation and scale types\n  // in theory the graph may support other types, but they\n  // have not been tested\n  mha_graph->set_io_data_type(dtype)\n      .set_intermediate_data_type(fe::DataType_t::FLOAT)\n      .set_compute_data_type(fe::DataType_t::FLOAT);\n  auto attn_scale =\n      mha_graph->tensor(fe::graph::Tensor_attributes()\n                            .set_uid(SCALE)\n                            .set_name(\"Attn_scale\")\n                            .set_dim({1, 1, 1, 1})\n                            .set_stride({1, 1, 1, 1})\n                            .set_is_pass_by_value(true)\n                            .set_data_type(fe::DataType_t::FLOAT));\n  auto sdpa_backward_options = fe::graph::SDPA_backward_attributes()\n                                   .set_name(\"CUDNN_SDPA_BACKWARD\")\n                                   .set_causal_mask(is_causal)\n                                   .set_attn_scale(attn_scale);\n  if (use_ragged_in_dense(q, k, v, o, attn_bias.has_value())) {\n    auto SEQ_LEN_Q_ =\n        mha_graph->tensor(fe::graph::Tensor_attributes()\n                              .set_uid(SEQ_LEN_Q)\n                              .set_name(\"Seq_q\")\n                              .set_dim({b, 1, 1, 1})\n                              .set_stride({1, 1, 1, 1})\n                              .set_data_type(fe::DataType_t::INT32));\n    auto SEQ_LEN_KV_ =\n        mha_graph->tensor(fe::graph::Tensor_attributes()\n                              .set_uid(SEQ_LEN_KV)\n                              .set_name(\"Seq_kv\")\n                              .set_dim({b, 1, 1, 1})\n                              .set_stride({1, 1, 1, 1})\n                              .set_data_type(fe::DataType_t::INT32));\n    sdpa_backward_options.set_seq_len_q(SEQ_LEN_Q_)\n        .set_seq_len_kv(SEQ_LEN_KV_)\n        .set_padding_mask(true);\n  }\n\n  auto Q_ = mha_graph->tensor(\n      fe::graph::Tensor_attributes().set_uid(Q).set_name(\"Q\"));\n  auto K_ = mha_graph->tensor(\n      fe::graph::Tensor_attributes().set_uid(K).set_name(\"K\"));\n  auto V_ = mha_graph->tensor(\n      fe::graph::Tensor_attributes().set_uid(V).set_name(\"V\"));\n  std::optional<std::shared_ptr<fe::graph::Tensor_attributes>> bias;\n  if (attn_bias.has_value()) {\n    bias =\n        mha_graph->tensor(fe::graph::Tensor_attributes()\n                              .set_uid(BIAS)\n                              .set_name(\"bias\")\n                              .set_dim(attn_bias.value().sizes().vec())\n                              .set_stride(attn_bias.value().strides().vec()));\n    sdpa_backward_options.set_bias(bias.value());\n  }\n  if (dropout_probability != 0.0f) {\n    auto seed = mha_graph->tensor(fe::graph::Tensor_attributes()\n                                      .set_uid(SEED)\n                                      .set_name(\"Seed\")\n                                      .set_dim({1, 1, 1, 1})\n                                      .set_stride({1, 1, 1, 1})\n                                      .set_data_type(\n                                          dropoutseed.dtype() == kInt\n                                              ? fe::DataType_t::INT32\n                                              : fe::DataType_t::INT64));\n    auto offset = mha_graph->tensor(fe::graph::Tensor_attributes()\n                                        .set_uid(OFFSET)\n                                        .set_name(\"Offset\")\n                                        .set_dim({1, 1, 1, 1})\n                                        .set_stride({1, 1, 1, 1})\n                                        .set_data_type(\n                                            dropoutoffset.dtype() == kInt\n                                                ? fe::DataType_t::INT32\n                                                : fe::DataType_t::INT64));\n    sdpa_backward_options.set_dropout(dropout_probability, seed, offset);\n  }\n  auto O_ = mha_graph->tensor(\n      fe::graph::Tensor_attributes().set_uid(O).set_name(\"O\"));\n  auto Stats = mha_graph->tensor(fe::graph::Tensor_attributes()\n                                     .set_uid(LSE)\n                                     .set_name(\"Stats\")\n                                     .set_stride(softmaxstats.strides().vec())\n                                     .set_data_type(fe::DataType_t::FLOAT));\n  auto Do = mha_graph->tensor(\n      fe::graph::Tensor_attributes().set_uid(DO).set_name(\"DO\"));\n  auto [Dq, Dk, Dv] = mha_graph->sdpa_backward(\n      Q_, K_, V_, O_, Do, Stats, sdpa_backward_options);\n  Dq->set_uid(DQ).set_output(true);\n  Dk->set_uid(DK).set_output(true);\n  Dv->set_uid(DV).set_output(true);\n  if (use_ragged_in_dense(q, k, v, o, attn_bias.has_value())) {\n    auto RAG_Q_OFF_ =\n        mha_graph->tensor(fe::graph::Tensor_attributes()\n                              .set_uid(RAG_Q_OFF)\n                              .set_name(\"cum_seq_q\")\n                              .set_dim({b + 1, 1, 1, 1})\n                              .set_stride({1, 1, 1, 1})\n                              .set_data_type(fe::DataType_t::INT32));\n    auto RAG_K_OFF_ =\n        mha_graph->tensor(fe::graph::Tensor_attributes()\n                              .set_uid(RAG_K_OFF)\n                              .set_name(\"cum_seq_k\")\n                              .set_dim({b + 1, 1, 1, 1})\n                              .set_stride({1, 1, 1, 1})\n                              .set_data_type(fe::DataType_t::INT32));\n    auto RAG_V_OFF_ =\n        mha_graph->tensor(fe::graph::Tensor_attributes()\n                              .set_uid(RAG_V_OFF)\n                              .set_name(\"cum_seq_v\")\n                              .set_dim({b + 1, 1, 1, 1})\n                              .set_stride({1, 1, 1, 1})\n                              .set_data_type(fe::DataType_t::INT32));\n    auto RAG_O_OFF_ =\n        mha_graph->tensor(fe::graph::Tensor_attributes()\n                              .set_uid(RAG_O_OFF)\n                              .set_name(\"cum_seq_o\")\n                              .set_dim({b + 1, 1, 1, 1})\n                              .set_stride({1, 1, 1, 1})\n                              .set_data_type(fe::DataType_t::INT32));\n    auto RAG_STATS_OFF_ =\n        mha_graph->tensor(fe::graph::Tensor_attributes()\n                              .set_uid(RAG_LSE_OFF)\n                              .set_name(\"cum_seq_stats\")\n Dv->set_ragged_offset(RAG_V_OFF_);\n    Do->set_ragged_offset(RAG_O_OFF_);\n    auto qsizevec = q.sizes().vec();\n    auto ksizevec = k.sizes().vec();\n    auto vsizevec = v.sizes().vec();\n    auto osizevec = o.sizes().vec();\n    qsizevec[2] = roundup_power2(qsizevec[2]);\n    ksizevec[2] = roundup_power2(ksizevec[2]);\n    vsizevec[2] = roundup_power2(vsizevec[2]);\n    osizevec[2] = roundup_power2(osizevec[2]);\n    // see corresponding section in the forward about the hardcoding\n    // of strides here\n    Q_->set_dim(qsizevec).set_stride(\n        {INT_MAX, qsizevec[3], qsizevec[1] * qsizevec[3], 1});\n    K_->set_dim(ksizevec).set_stride(\n        {INT_MAX, ksizevec[3], ksizevec[1] * ksizevec[3], 1});\n    V_->set_dim(vsizevec).set_stride(\n        {INT_MAX, vsizevec[3], vsizevec[1] * vsizevec[3], 1});\n    O_->set_dim(osizevec).set_stride(\n        {INT_MAX, osizevec[3], osizevec[1] * osizevec[3], 1});\n    // should be identical to their non-d counterparts\n    Dq->set_dim(qsizevec).set_stride(\n        {INT_MAX, qsizevec[3], qsizevec[1] * qsizevec[3], 1});\n    Dk->set_dim(ksizevec).set_stride(\n        {INT_MAX, ksizevec[3], ksizevec[1] * ksizevec[3], 1});\n    Dv->set_dim(vsizevec).set_stride(\n        {INT_MAX, vsizevec[3], vsizevec[1] * vsizevec[3], 1});\n    Do->set_dim(osizevec).set_stride(\n        {INT_MAX, osizevec[3], osizevec[1] * osizevec[3], 1});\n\n    Stats->set_ragged_offset(RAG_STATS_OFF_);\n    auto statssizevec = softmaxstats.sizes().vec();\n    statssizevec[2] = roundup_power2(statssizevec[2]);\n    Stats->set_dim(statssizevec);\n  } else {\n    O_->set_dim(o.sizes().vec()).set_stride(o.strides().vec());\n    Q_->set_dim(q.sizes().vec()).set_stride(q.strides().vec());\n    K_->set_dim(k.sizes().vec()).set_stride(k.strides().vec());\n    V_->set_dim(v.sizes().vec()).set_stride(v.strides().vec());\n    Dq->set_dim(dQ.sizes().vec()).set_stride(dQ.strides().vec());\n    Dk->set_dim(dK.sizes().vec()).set_stride(dK.strides().vec());\n    Dv->set_dim(dV.sizes().vec()).set_stride(dV.strides().vec());\n    Do->set_dim(dO.sizes().vec()).set_stride(dO.strides().vec());\n    Stats->set_dim(softmaxstats.sizes().vec());\n  }\n\n  AT_CUDNN_FRONTEND_CHECK(mha_graph->validate());\n  AT_CUDNN_FRONTEND_CHECK(mha_graph->build_operation_graph(handle));\n  AT_CUDNN_FRONTEND_CHECK(\n      mha_graph->create_execution_plans({fe::HeurMode_t::A}));\n  AT_CUDNN_FRONTEND_CHECK(mha_graph->check_support(handle));\n  AT_CUDNN_FRONTEND_CHECK(mha_graph->build_plans(handle));\n  return mha_graph;\n}\n\nauto build_graph_backward_nestedtensor(\n    int64_t b,\n    int64_t h_q,\n    int64_t h_k,\n    int64_t h_v,\n               .set_dim(attn_bias.value().sizes().vec())\n                              .set_stride(attn_bias.value().strides().vec()));\n    sdpa_backward_options.set_bias(bias.value());\n  }\n  auto
